\doxysubsection*{Modules}
\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\textbf{ Core Debug Registers (\+Core\+Debug)}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Cortex-\/\+M0 Core Debug Registers (DCB registers, SHCSR, and DFSR) are only accessible over DAP and not via processor. Therefore they are not covered by the Cortex-\/\+M0 header file. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
\doxysubsection*{Data Structures}
\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
